My experience at Escape This was very good. I enjoy doing escape rooms with friends and what better than to do one down the street from where you live. The prices aren't too expensive. <gmap_id>0x808f7dcc1dbccdb9:0xc1a998542d93ede2</gmap_id>< review>
SO happy that I found this place during quarantine. I saw a photo of their cheong fun on instagram and was excited that this place was located near me. I've been here countless times since prices are cheap and affordable. They're fast and the food tastes great. Should note that they take cash only, but I think they accept venmo as well. I've tried their cheong fun with shrimp, beef, egg and corn, and liver. All of them have been great and I love this style of cheong fun, where the toppings are on top, rather than inside. I've also tried their pan fried noodles. They kept the sauce and noodles separate which I greatly appreciated. The noodles were fresh and super crispy. Their salt and pepper wings are also full of flavor and a great snack. I would highly  recommend this place!<//review>

< review>
Cash only to be prepped and brought over!

I haven't had Hong Kong cafe grub food for days and this simply just hits the spot!

Their rice noodle rolls are delicious and so fresh with complimenting squishable bottled sweet soy sauce to go squirt all over it!  They have many fillings to choose from and my favorite was the shrimp and beef!

They have the signature stir fried dishes that's superbly bomb and homely!  Picture foods on the wall to choose from.

Hong Kong iced milk tea for the refreshing win!

I was in a happy place grubbing and munching!< /review>

<text>New establishment located on Ocean Avenue near 24 Hour gym and next to Emma's restaurant. There rice porridge/ conger is pretty good. Size is personal sized for all porridge items. <Rating>4</Rating><review>For their Taco Tuesday:

My top 2 tacos were: spicy ahi with Thai basil and the chicken wing with Thai slaw over the Thai larb with ground chicken and the crispy white fish with Thai slaw and avocado.   As for the duck and crispy pork belly taco, I'm sure it would be tasty and make for a great picture.

< Text>
When driving from Phoenix to LA, this is always one of my stops.  It is convenient, always clean, and my truck gets better mileage on their gas.   They do offer both regular gas and deisel at fair rates.  The store contains everything you expect from a gas station convenience store, along with slot machines.  The outside restrooms are only open during the day.  At night you will need to use the restrooms inside the store, if needed.

Nearby you have food options such as Panda Express, Taco Bell, and Ruby Tuesday.  There is also a 24-hour Starbucks, which is a godsend on long trips.< /Text>
